==========================The_first_checker_query=========================
You are an expert in writing java rule checkers and I need your help to generate a custom java rule checker in PMD tool version 7.0.0. 
I will give you a rule description, which may contain multiple violations. You just need to generate a checker that can check the violations of the given test case.

The following is a description of the rule and the corresponding counterexample test case and the AST of the counterexample test case:

Rule description: The use of the ‘+=’ operator for appending strings causes the JVM to create and use an internal StringBuffer. If it is used more than once then the explicit use of a StringBuilder or threadsafe StringBuffer is recommended to avoid this.;
The test case corresponding to the rule:
```
// failure case
package xxx;
public class Foo {
    public void bar() {
        String x;
        x = "foo";
        x += "bar";
        x += "baz";
    }
}
The description of this test case is: bad 1
The number of violating the rule in this test case is: 2

```

==========5轮中每一轮为第一个测试用例生成的checker===============
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;

import java.util.*;

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.getText().equals("+=")) {
            ASTExpression leftOperand = node.getLeftOperand();
            ASTExpression rightOperand = node.getRightOperand();

            if (leftOperand instanceof ASTVariableAccess && rightOperand instanceof ASTStringLiteral) {
                ASTVariableAccess variableAccess = (ASTVariableAccess) leftOperand;
                ASTStringLiteral stringLiteral = (ASTStringLiteral) rightOperand;

                if (variableAccess.getText().equals("x") && stringLiteral.isStringLiteral()) {
                    addViolation(data, node);
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

==========5轮中每一轮为第一个测试用例生成的checker===============
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;

import java.util.*;
import java.lang.*;

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.getText().equals("+=")) {
            ASTVariableAccess variableAccess = node.firstChild(ASTVariableAccess.class);
            if (variableAccess != null && variableAccess.getText().equals("x")) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

        super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
    }

    }

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;

import java.util.*;
import java.lang.*;

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.PLUS_ASSIGN) {
            ASTVariableAccess variableAccess = node.getFirstChildOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class);
            if (variableAccess != null && variableAccess.getType() != null && variableAccess.getType().isString()) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.PLUS_ASSIGN && JavaAstUtils.isStringConcatExpr(node.getRightOperand())) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.getOperator() == JavaTokenKinds.PLUS_ASSIGN && JavaAstUtils.isStringConcatExpr(node.getRightOperand())) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

==========5轮中每一轮为第一个测试用例生成的checker===============
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;

import java.util.*;
import java.lang.*;

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.PLUS_ASSIGN) {
            ASTVariableAccess varAccess = node.getLeftOperand().firstChild(ASTVariableAccess.class);
            if (varAccess != null) {
                String varName = varAccess.getName();
                int count = countPlusAssignments(node, varName);
                if (count > 1) {
                    addViolation(data, node);
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    private int countPlusAssignments(ASTAssignmentExpression node, String varName) {
        int count = 0;
        ASTBlock block = node.ancestors(ASTBlock.class).first();
        if (block != null) {
            for (ASTExpressionStatement stmt : block.children(ASTExpressionStatement.class)) {
                ASTAssignmentExpression assignment = stmt.firstChild(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
                if (assignment != null && assignment.getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.PLUS_ASSIGN) {
                    ASTVariableAccess access = assignment.getLeftOperand().firstChild(ASTVariableAccess.class);
                    if (access != null && varName.equals(access.getName())) {
                        count++;
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        return count;
    }
}

==========================第2轮为第一个测试用例生成checker========================
=========================logics=========================
1. Get all assignment expressions in the constructor.
2. Check whether the operator in the assignment expression is `+=`.
3. Get the left-hand side operand of the assignment expression.
4. Check whether the left-hand side operand is a string type.
5. Count the number of `+=` operations on string types.

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.PLUS_ASSIGN) {
            NodeStream<ASTVariableAccess> leftOperands = node.getLeftOperand().descendants(ASTVariableAccess.class);
            for (ASTVariableAccess leftOperand : leftOperands) {
                if ("x".equals(leftOperand.getName())) {
                    addViolation(data, node);
                    break; // No need to check further if we found a violation
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

==========5轮中每一轮为第一个测试用例生成的checker===============
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;

import java.util.*;

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.PLUS_ASSIGN) {
            ASTAssignableExpr leftOperand = node.getLeftOperand();
            if (leftOperand instanceof ASTVariableAccess) {
                ASTVariableAccess varAccess = (ASTVariableAccess) leftOperand;
                String varName = varAccess.getName();
                NodeStream<ASTAssignmentExpression> assignments = node.getParent().descendants(ASTAssignmentExpression.class)
                    .filter(assign -> assign.getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.PLUS_ASSIGN)
                    .filter(assign -> {
                        ASTAssignableExpr left = assign.getLeftOperand();
                        return left instanceof ASTVariableAccess && ((ASTVariableAccess) left).getName().equals(varName);
                    });

                if (assignments.count() > 1) {
                    addViolation(data, node);
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

==========5轮中每一轮为第一个测试用例生成的checker===============
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;

import java.util.*;
import java.lang.*;

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.PLUS_ASSIGNMENT) {
            JavaNode leftOperand = node.getLeftOperand();
            if (leftOperand instanceof ASTVariableAccess) {
                ASTVariableAccess variableAccess = (ASTVariableAccess) leftOperand;
                String variableName = variableAccess.getName();
                int count = countStringAppends(variableName, node);
                if (count > 1) {
                    addViolation(data, node);
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    private int countStringAppends(String variableName, ASTAssignmentExpression node) {
        int count = 0;
        ASTBlock block = node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTBlock.class);
        if (block != null) {
            for (ASTExpressionStatement statement : block.descendants(ASTExpressionStatement.class)) {
                ASTAssignmentExpression assignment = statement.getFirstChildOfType(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
                if (assignment != null && assignment.getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.PLUS_ASSIGNMENT) {
                    ASTVariableAccess access = assignment.getLeftOperand().getFirstChildOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class);
                    if (access != null && variableName.equals(access.getName())) {
                        count++;
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        return count;
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;

import java.util.*;
import java.lang.*;

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.PLUS_ASSIGNMENT) {
            NodeStream<ASTVariableAccess> variableAccesses = node.descendants(ASTVariableAccess.class);
            for (ASTVariableAccess variableAccess : variableAccesses) {
                if (variableAccess.getText().equals("x")) {
                    addViolation(data, node);
                    break; // No need to check further if we found a violation
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.PLUS_ASSIGNMENT) {
            NodeStream<ASTVariableAccess> variableAccesses = node.descendants(ASTVariableAccess.class);
            if (variableAccesses.count() > 1) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;

import java.util.*;
import java.lang.*;

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.PLUS_ASSIGNMENT) {
            ASTVariableAccess varAccess = node.getFirstChildOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class);
            if (varAccess != null && varAccess.getType() != null && varAccess.getType().isClass() && varAccess.getType().getSymbol().getName().equals("String")) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.PLUS_ASSIGNMENT) {
            NodeStream<ASTAssignmentExpression> assignments = node.ancestorsOrSelf()
                .filterIs(ASTAssignmentExpression.class)
                .filter(n -> n.getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.PLUS_ASSIGNMENT);

            if (assignments.count() > 1) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

            result += i;
        }
    }

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.PLUS_ASSIGN || node.getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.ASSIGN) {
            ASTExpression rightOperand = node.getRightOperand();
            if (JavaAstUtils.isStringConcatExpr(rightOperand)) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

==========================第3轮为第一个测试用例生成checker========================
=========================logics=========================
1. Get all assignment expressions in the method.
2. Check whether the operator in the assignment expression is `+=`.
3. Check whether the left-hand side operand of the assignment expression is a string type.
4. Check whether the right-hand side operand of the assignment expression is a string type.

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.getText().equals("+=")) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

==========5轮中每一轮为第一个测试用例生成的checker===============
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;

import java.util.*;
import java.lang.*;

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.getOperator() == JavaTokenKinds.PLUS_ASSIGN || node.getOperator() == JavaTokenKinds.PLUS) {
            if (node.getLeftOperand() instanceof ASTVariableAccess) {
                ASTVariableAccess leftOperand = (ASTVariableAccess) node.getLeftOperand();
                if (leftOperand.getType() != null && leftOperand.getType().isString()) {
                    addViolation(data, node);
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.PLUS_ASSIGNMENT || node.getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.PLUS) {
            if (node.getLeftOperand() instanceof ASTVariableAccess) {
                ASTVariableAccess leftOperand = (ASTVariableAccess) node.getLeftOperand();
                if (leftOperand.getName().equals("result")) {
                    addViolation(data, node);
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

You are an expert in writing java rule checkers and I need your help to generate a custom java rule checker in PMD tool version 7.0.0. 
I will give you a rule description, which may contain multiple violations. You just need to generate a checker that can check the violations of the given test case.

The following is a description of the rule and the corresponding counterexample test case and the AST of the counterexample test case:

Rule description: The use of the ‘+=’ operator for appending strings causes the JVM to create and use an internal StringBuffer. If it is used more than once then the explicit use of a StringBuilder or threadsafe StringBuffer is recommended to avoid this.;
The test case corresponding to the rule:
```
// violation: concat to String in for/while loop
import java.util.*;

public class ConcatInLoop {

    public void bad1() {
        String logStatement = "";
        List<String> values = Arrays.asList("tic", "tac", "toe");
        for (String val : values) {
            logStatement = logStatement + val + ", "; // bad
        }
        Iterator iter = values.iterator();
        while (iter.hasNext()) {
            logStatement = logStatement + iter.next() + ", "; // bad
        }
    }
    public void bad2() {
        String log = "";
        List<String> values = Arrays.asList("tic", "tac", "toe");
        for (String val1 : values) {
            log += val1; // bad
        }
        for (String val2 : values) log += val2; // bad
    }

    public void bad3() {
        String logStatement = "";
        List<String> values = Arrays.asList("tic", "tac", "toe");
        for (String val : values) {
            logStatement += val + ", "; // bad
        }
    }
}
The description of this test case is: bad 6
The number of violating the rule in this test case is: 5

==========5轮中每一轮为第一个测试用例生成的checker===============
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class, ASTForeachStatement.class, ASTWhileStatement.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        if (JavaAstUtils.isStringConcatExpr(node.getRightOperand())) {
            ASTAssignableExpr leftOperand = node.getLeftOperand();
            if (leftOperand instanceof ASTVariableAccess) {
                ASTVariableAccess varAccess = (ASTVariableAccess) leftOperand;
                if (varAccess.getType() != null && varAccess.getType().isString()) {
                    addViolation(data, node);
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTForeachStatement node, Object data) {
        node.getBody().accept(this, data);
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTWhileStatement node, Object data) {
        node.getBody().accept(this, data);
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

==========5轮中每一轮为第一个测试用例生成的checker===============
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.PLUS_ASSIGNMENT || node.getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.ASSIGNMENT) {
            if (JavaAstUtils.isStringConcatExpr(node.getRightOperand())) {
                NodeStream<ASTVariableAccess> variableAccesses = node.getRightOperand().descendants(ASTVariableAccess.class);
                for (ASTVariableAccess varAccess : variableAccesses) {
                    if (varAccess.getReferencedName().equals(node.getLeftOperand().getVarId().getName())) {
                        addViolation(data, node);
                        break;
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

You are an expert in writing java rule checkers and I need your help to generate a custom java rule checker in PMD tool version 7.0.0. 
I will give you a rule description, which may contain multiple violations. You just need to generate a checker that can check the violations of the given test case.

The following is a description of the rule and the corresponding counterexample test case and the AST of the counterexample test case:

Rule description: The use of the ‘+=’ operator for appending strings causes the JVM to create and use an internal StringBuffer. If it is used more than once then the explicit use of a StringBuilder or threadsafe StringBuffer is recommended to avoid this.;
The test case corresponding to the rule:
```
// violation: concat to String in for/while loop
import java.util.*;

public class ConcatInLoop {

    public void bad1() {
        String logStatement = "";
        List<String> values = Arrays.asList("tic", "tac", "toe");
        for (String val : values) {
            logStatement = logStatement + val + ", "; // bad
        }
        Iterator iter = values.iterator();
        while (iter.hasNext()) {
            logStatement = logStatement + iter.next() + ", "; // bad
        }
    }
    public void bad2() {
        String log = "";
        List<String> values = Arrays.asList("tic", "tac", "toe");
        for (String val1 : values) {
            log += val1; // bad
        }
        for (String val2 : values) log += val2; // bad
    }

    public void bad3() {
        String logStatement = "";
        List<String> values = Arrays.asList("tic", "tac", "toe");
        for (String val : values) {
            logStatement += val + ", "; // bad
        }
    }
}
The description of this test case is: bad 6
The number of violating the rule in this test case is: 5

```

==========5轮中每一轮为第一个测试用例生成的checker===============
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class, ASTForeachStatement.class, ASTWhileStatement.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        if (JavaAstUtils.isStringConcatExpr(node.getRightOperand())) {
            ASTAssignableExpr leftOperand = node.getLeftOperand();
            if (leftOperand instanceof ASTVariableAccess) {
                ASTVariableAccess varAccess = (ASTVariableAccess) leftOperand;
                if (varAccess.getType() != null && varAccess.getType().isString()) {
                    addViolation(data, node);
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTForeachStatement node, Object data) {
        node.getBody().accept(this, data);
        return data;
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTWhileStatement node, Object data) {
        node.getBody().accept(this, data);
        return data;
    }
}

5. Count the number of violations where the `+=` operator is used for appending strings inside a loop.

The following is a description of the rule and the corresponding counterexample test case and the AST of the counterexample test case:

Rule description: The use of the ‘+=’ operator for appending strings causes the JVM to create and use an internal StringBuffer. If it is used more than once then the explicit use of a StringBuilder or threadsafe StringBuffer is recommended to avoid this.;
The test case corresponding to the rule:
```
// violation: concat to String in for/while loop
import java.util.*;

public class ConcatInLoop {

    public void bad1() {
        String logStatement = "";
        List<String> values = Arrays.asList("tic", "tac", "toe");
        for (String val : values) {
            logStatement = logStatement + val + ", "; // bad
        }
        Iterator iter = values.iterator();
        while (iter.hasNext()) {
            logStatement = logStatement + iter.next() + ", "; // bad
        }
    }
    public void bad2() {
        String log = "";
        List<String> values = Arrays.asList("tic", "tac", "toe");
        for (String val1 : values) {
            log += val1; // bad
        }
        for (String val2 : values) log += val2; // bad
    }

    public void bad3() {
        String logStatement = "";
        List<String> values = Arrays.asList("tic", "tac", "toe");
        for (String val : values) {
            logStatement += val + ", "; // bad
        }
    }
}
The description of this test case is: bad 6
The number of violating the rule in this test case is: 5

==========5轮中每一轮为第一个测试用例生成的checker===============
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.PLUS_ASSIGN || node.getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.PLUS) {
            NodeStream<ASTVariableAccess> variableAccesses = node.descendants(ASTVariableAccess.class);
            for (ASTVariableAccess varAccess : variableAccesses) {
                if (varAccess.getType() != null && varAccess.getType().isString()) {
                    addViolation(data, node);
                    break;
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

   - In the second `for` loop, `log += val2` violates the rule (`+=` operator for string concatenation in a loop).

==========5轮中每一轮为第一个测试用例生成的checker===============
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;

import java.util.*;
import java.lang.*;

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.PLUS_ASSIGN || node.getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.PLUS) {
            ASTVariableAccess leftOperand = node.getFirstChildOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class);
            if (leftOperand != null && leftOperand.getType() != null && leftOperand.getType().isClass(String.class)) {
                ASTBlockStatement blockStatement = node.getFirstParentOfType(ASTBlockStatement.class);
                if (blockStatement != null) {
                    ASTBlock block = blockStatement.getFirstParentOfType(ASTBlock.class);
                    if (block != null) {
                        ASTStatement statement = blockStatement.getFirstParentOfType(ASTStatement.class);
                        if (statement != null) {
                            ASTStatement parentStatement = statement.getFirstParentOfType(ASTStatement.class);
                            if (parentStatement instanceof ASTForeachStatement || parentStatement instanceof ASTWhileStatement) {
                                addViolation(data, node);
                            }
                        }
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

==========================The_first_checker_query=========================
You are an expert in writing java rule checkers and I need your help to generate a custom java rule checker in PMD tool version 7.0.0. 
I will give you a rule description, which may contain multiple violations. You just need to generate a checker that can check the violations of the given test case.

The following is a description of the rule and the corresponding counterexample test case and the AST of the counterexample test case:

Rule description: The use of the ‘+=’ operator for appending strings causes the JVM to create and use an internal StringBuffer. If it is used more than once then the explicit use of a StringBuilder or threadsafe StringBuffer is recommended to avoid this.;
The test case corresponding to the rule:
```
// violation: various concats in loop
import java.util.*;

public class ConcatInLoop {
    public String bad() {
        String description = " " + ";";
        List<String> persons = new ArrayList<String>();
        for (final String person : persons) {
            if (person != null) {
                description += "0" + ":"; //bad
            } else {
                description += ":"; //bad
            }
            description += person.toString() + ":"; // bad
            description += ";"; // bad
            description += person.toString(); // bad
        }
        return description;
    }
}
The description of this test case is: bad 7
The number of violating the rule in this test case is: 5

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;

import java.util.*;
import java.lang.*;

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.PLUS_ASSIGN) {
            ASTVariableAccess varAccess = node.getLeftOperand().firstChild(ASTVariableAccess.class);
            if (varAccess != null && "description".equals(varAccess.getName())) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.PLUS_ASSIGN) {
            ASTVariableAccess variableAccess = node.getLeftOperand().firstChild(ASTVariableAccess.class);
            if (variableAccess != null && "description".equals(variableAccess.getName())) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

            description += person.toString() + ":"; // bad
            description += ";"; // bad
            description += person.toString(); // bad
        }
        return description;
    }

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.PLUS_ASSIGNMENT) {
            NodeStream<ASTVariableAccess> variableAccesses = node.descendants(ASTVariableAccess.class);
            for (ASTVariableAccess varAccess : variableAccesses) {
                if (varAccess.getReferencedName().equals("description")) {
                    addViolation(data, node);
                    break;
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.getOperator() == JavaTokenKind.PLUS_ASSIGN) {
            ASTExpression rightOperand = node.getRightOperand();
            if (JavaAstUtils.isStringConcatExpr(rightOperand)) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

// violation: various concats in loop
import java.util.*;

public class ConcatInLoop {
    public String bad() {
        String description = " " + ";";
        List<String> persons = new ArrayList<String>();
        for (final String person : persons) {
            if (person != null) {
                description += "0" + ":"; //bad
            } else {
                description += ":"; //bad
            }
            description += person.toString() + ":"; // bad
            description += ";"; // bad
            description += person.toString(); // bad
        }
        return description;
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;

import java.util.*;
import java.lang.*;

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        if (node.getText().contains("+=")) {
            ASTVariableAccess varAccess = node.getFirstChildOfType(ASTVariableAccess.class);
            if (varAccess != null && varAccess.getText().equals("description")) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

==========5轮中每一轮为第一个测试用例生成的checker===============
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTDoStatement.class, ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTDoStatement node, Object data) {
        NodeStream<ASTAssignmentExpression> assignments = node.descendants(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
        for (ASTAssignmentExpression assignment : assignments) {
            if (JavaAstUtils.isStringConcatExpr(assignment.getRightOperand())) {
                addViolation(data, assignment);
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        if (JavaAstUtils.isStringConcatExpr(node.getRightOperand())) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

Rule description: The use of the ‘+=’ operator for appending strings causes the JVM to create and use an internal StringBuffer. If it is used more than once then the explicit use of a StringBuilder or threadsafe StringBuffer is recommended to avoid this.;

// violation: concat to String in do-loop

public class ConcatInLoop {

    public void bad() {
        String logStatement = "";

        int i = 0;
        do {
            logStatement = logStatement + values.get(i++) + ", "; // bad
        } while (i < values.length());
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTDoStatement.class, ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTDoStatement node, Object data) {
        node.getBody().accept(this, data);
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        if (JavaAstUtils.isStringConcatExpr(node.getRightOperand())) {
            ASTVariableAccess leftOperand = node.getLeftOperand().firstChild(ASTVariableAccess.class);
            if (leftOperand != null && "logStatement".equals(leftOperand.getName())) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

The following is a description of the rule and the corresponding counterexample test case and the AST of the counterexample test case:

Rule description: The use of the ‘+=’ operator for appending strings causes the JVM to create and use an internal StringBuffer. If it is used more than once then the explicit use of a StringBuilder or threadsafe StringBuffer is recommended to avoid this.;
The test case corresponding to the rule:
```
// violation: concat to String in do-loop
import java.util.*;

public class ConcatInLoop {

    public void bad() {
        String logStatement = "";
        List<String> values = Arrays.asList("tic", "tac", "toe");
        int i = 0;
        do {
            logStatement = logStatement + values.get(i++) + ", "; // bad
        } while (i < values.length());
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class, ASTDoStatement.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        if (JavaAstUtils.isStringConcatExpr(node.getRightOperand())) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTDoStatement node, Object data) {
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

================修复新加测试用例后生成的checker===================
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class, ASTDoStatement.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        if (JavaAstUtils.isStringConcatExpr(node.getRightOperand())) {
            ASTAssignableExpr leftOperand = node.getLeftOperand();
            if (leftOperand instanceof ASTVariableAccess) {
                ASTVariableAccess varAccess = (ASTVariableAccess) leftOperand;
                NodeStream<ASTAssignmentExpression> assignments = node.getParent().getParent().descendants(ASTAssignmentExpression.class)
                    .filter(assign -> {
                        ASTAssignableExpr assignLeft = assign.getLeftOperand();
                        return assignLeft instanceof ASTVariableAccess && ((ASTVariableAccess) assignLeft).getName().equals(varAccess.getName());
                    });

                if (assignments.count() > 1) {
                    addViolation(data, node);
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTDoStatement node, Object data) {
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class, ASTDoStatement.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        if (JavaAstUtils.isStringConcatExpr(node.getRightOperand())) {
            NodeStream<ASTAssignmentExpression> assignments = node.getParents().ancestors(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
            if (assignments.noneMatch(assign -> assign.getLeftOperand().equals(node.getLeftOperand()))) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTDoStatement node, Object data) {
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class, ASTDoStatement.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        if (JavaAstUtils.isStringConcatExpr(node.getRightOperand())) {
            NodeStream<ASTAssignmentExpression> assignments = node.getParent().descendants(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
            int count = assignments.filter(assign -> assign.getLeftOperand() instanceof ASTVariableAccess && 
                                                    ((ASTVariableAccess) assign.getLeftOperand()).getVariableName().equals(((ASTVariableAccess) node.getLeftOperand()).getVariableName()) && 
                                                    JavaAstUtils.isStringConcatExpr(assign.getRightOperand())).count();
            if (count > 1) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTDoStatement node, Object data) {
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class, ASTDoStatement.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        if (JavaAstUtils.isStringConcatExpr(node.getRightOperand())) {
            NodeStream<ASTAssignmentExpression> assignments = node.getParent().ancestors(ASTBlock.class)
                .first()
                .descendants(ASTAssignmentExpression.class)
                .filter(assign -> assign.getLeftOperand() instanceof ASTVariableAccess
                    && ((ASTVariableAccess) assign.getLeftOperand()).getName().equals(((ASTVariableAccess) node.getLeftOperand()).getName()));
            if (assignments.count() > 1) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTDoStatement node, Object data) {
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class, ASTDoStatement.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        if (JavaAstUtils.isStringConcatExpr(node.getRightOperand())) {
            NodeStream<ASTAssignmentExpression> assignments = node.getParent().descendants(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
            int count = assignments.filter(assign -> assign.getLeftOperand() instanceof ASTVariableAccess 
                    && ((ASTVariableAccess) assign.getLeftOperand()).getName().equals(((ASTVariableAccess) node.getLeftOperand()).getName()) 
                    && JavaAstUtils.isStringConcatExpr(assign.getRightOperand())).count();
            if (count > 1) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTDoStatement node, Object data) {
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

You are an expert in writing java rule checkers in PMD tool version 7.0.0. 
You have helped me write a checker for this rule:
Rule description: The use of the ‘+=’ operator for appending strings causes the JVM to create and use an internal StringBuffer. If it is used more than once then the explicit use of a StringBuilder or threadsafe StringBuffer is recommended to avoid this.;
And the source code of the checker is as follows:
```
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class, ASTDoStatement.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        if (JavaAstUtils.isStringConcatExpr(node.getRightOperand())) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTDoStatement node, Object data) {
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}
```

import java.util.*;

public class ConcatInLoop {

    public void bad() {
        String logStatement = "";
        List<String> values = Arrays.asList("tic", "tac", "toe");
        int i = 0;
        do {
            logStatement = logStatement + values.get(i++) + ", "; // bad
        } while (i < values.length());
    }
}

// Test new rule example
public class Foo {
                String inefficientConcatenation() {
                    String result = "";
                    for (int i = 0; i < 10; i++) {
                        // warning: this concatenation will create one new StringBuilder per iteration
                        result += getStringFromSomeWhere(i);
                    }
                    return result;
                }

                String efficientConcatenation() {
                    // better would be to use one StringBuilder for the entire loop
                    StringBuilder result = new StringBuilder();
                    for (int i = 0; i < 10; i++) {
                        result.append(getStringFromSomeWhere(i));
                    }
                    return result.toString();
                }

                String getStringFromSomeWhere(int i) {
                    return "a" + i;
                }
            }

You are an expert in writing java rule checkers in PMD tool version 7.0.0. 
You have helped me write a checker for this rule:
Rule description: The use of the ‘+=’ operator for appending strings causes the JVM to create and use an internal StringBuffer. If it is used more than once then the explicit use of a StringBuilder or threadsafe StringBuffer is recommended to avoid this.;
And the source code of the checker is as follows:
```
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class, ASTDoStatement.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        if (JavaAstUtils.isStringConcatExpr(node.getRightOperand())) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTDoStatement node, Object data) {
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}
```

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class, ASTForStatement.class, ASTDoStatement.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        if (JavaAstUtils.isStringConcatExpr(node.getRightOperand())) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTForStatement node, Object data) {
        NodeStream<ASTAssignmentExpression> assignments = node.descendants(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
        for (ASTAssignmentExpression assignment : assignments) {
            if (JavaAstUtils.isStringConcatExpr(assignment.getRightOperand())) {
                addViolation(data, assignment);
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTDoStatement node, Object data) {
        NodeStream<ASTAssignmentExpression> assignments = node.descendants(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
        for (ASTAssignmentExpression assignment : assignments) {
            if (JavaAstUtils.isStringConcatExpr(assignment.getRightOperand())) {
                addViolation(data, assignment);
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class, ASTDoStatement.class, ASTForStatement.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        if (JavaAstUtils.isStringConcatExpr(node.getRightOperand())) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTDoStatement node, Object data) {
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTForStatement node, Object data) {
        NodeStream<ASTStatement> statements = node.getBody().children(ASTStatement.class);
        for (ASTStatement statement : statements) {
            if (statement instanceof ASTExpressionStatement) {
                ASTExpressionStatement exprStmt = (ASTExpressionStatement) statement;
                if (exprStmt.getExpr() instanceof ASTAssignmentExpression) {
                    ASTAssignmentExpression assignment = (ASTAssignmentExpression) exprStmt.getExpr();
                    if (JavaAstUtils.isStringConcatExpr(assignment.getRightOperand())) {
                        addViolation(data, assignment);
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

                        // warning: this concatenation will create one new StringBuilder per iteration

                    }
                    return result;

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class, ASTDoStatement.class, ASTForStatement.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        if (JavaAstUtils.isStringConcatExpr(node.getRightOperand())) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTDoStatement node, Object data) {
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTForStatement node, Object data) {
        NodeStream<ASTAssignmentExpression> assignments = node.descendants(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
        for (ASTAssignmentExpression assignment : assignments) {
            if (JavaAstUtils.isStringConcatExpr(assignment.getRightOperand())) {
                addViolation(data, assignment);
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

================修复新加测试用例后生成的checker===================
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class, ASTDoStatement.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        if (JavaAstUtils.isStringConcatExpr(node.getRightOperand())) {
            NodeStream<ASTVariableAccess> variableAccesses = node.getRightOperand().descendants(ASTVariableAccess.class);
            if (variableAccesses.anyMatch(va -> va.getReferencedSym().equals(node.getLeftOperand().getReferencedSym()))) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTDoStatement node, Object data) {
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class, ASTDoStatement.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        if (JavaAstUtils.isStringConcatExpr(node.getRightOperand())) {
            NodeStream<ASTVariableAccess> variableAccesses = node.descendants(ASTVariableAccess.class);
            if (variableAccesses.anyMatch(va -> va.getReferencedSym() != null && va.getReferencedSym().equals(((ASTVariableAccess) node.getLeftOperand()).getReferencedSym()))) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTDoStatement node, Object data) {
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

================修复新加测试用例后生成的checker===================
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class, ASTDoStatement.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        if (JavaAstUtils.isStringConcatExpr(node.getRightOperand())) {
            NodeStream<ASTAssignmentExpression> assignments = node.getParent()
                .descendants(ASTAssignmentExpression.class)
                .filter(assign -> assign.getLeftOperand() instanceof ASTVariableAccess
                    && ((ASTVariableAccess) assign.getLeftOperand()).getReferencedSym() == ((ASTVariableAccess) node.getLeftOperand()).getReferencedSym());

            if (assignments.count() > 1) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTDoStatement node, Object data) {
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class, ASTDoStatement.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        if (JavaAstUtils.isStringConcatExpr(node.getRightOperand())) {
            NodeStream<ASTAssignmentExpression> assignments = node.getParent().descendants(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
            if (assignments.count() > 1) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTDoStatement node, Object data) {
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class, ASTDoStatement.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        if (JavaAstUtils.isStringConcatExpr(node.getRightOperand())) {
            NodeStream<ASTAssignmentExpression> assignments = node.getParents()
                .ancestors(ASTBlock.class)
                .descendants(ASTAssignmentExpression.class)
                .filter(assign -> assign.getLeftOperand().equals(node.getLeftOperand()));
            
            if (assignments.count() > 1) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTDoStatement node, Object data) {
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

You are an expert in writing java rule checkers in PMD tool version 7.0.0. 
You have helped me write a checker for this rule:
Rule description: The use of the ‘+=’ operator for appending strings causes the JVM to create and use an internal StringBuffer. If it is used more than once then the explicit use of a StringBuilder or threadsafe StringBuffer is recommended to avoid this.;
And the source code of the checker is as follows:
```
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class, ASTDoStatement.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        if (JavaAstUtils.isStringConcatExpr(node.getRightOperand())) {
            addViolation(data, node);
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTDoStatement node, Object data) {
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}
```

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class, ASTDoStatement.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        if (JavaAstUtils.isStringConcatExpr(node.getRightOperand())) {
            NodeStream<ASTAssignmentExpression> assignments = node.getParents().ancestors(ASTAssignmentExpression.class);
            if (assignments.count() > 1) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTDoStatement node, Object data) {
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

================修复新加测试用例后生成的checker===================
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.performance;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public UseStringBufferForStringAppendsRule() {
        super(ASTAssignmentExpression.class, ASTDoStatement.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTAssignmentExpression node, Object data) {
        if (JavaAstUtils.isStringConcatExpr(node.getRightOperand())) {
            NodeStream<ASTAssignmentExpression> assignments = node.getParent()
                .ancestors(ASTBlock.class)
                .first()
                .descendants(ASTAssignmentExpression.class)
                .filter(assign -> assign.getLeftOperand().getText().equals(node.getLeftOperand().getText()));

            if (assignments.count() > 1) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTDoStatement node, Object data) {
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}
